  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_691d3056-030b-4642-92ee-508ac424c972'
      });
    }
    
    var initializeSiwa = function() {
      var APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL =  "https://appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js"
      loadScript(APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL, initAppleId);
    };

      initAppleId();
    } else {
      initializeSiwa();
    }

  <span id="freeText1778616140878505944" style="display:none">Kate Daniels works for the Order of the Knights of Merciful Aid, officially as a liaison with the mercenary guild. Unofficially, she cleans up the paranormal problems no one else wants to handle—especially if they involve Atlanta’s shapeshifting community.<br /><br />When she’s called in to investigate a fight at the Steel Horse, a bar midway between the territories of the shapeshifters and the necromancers, Kate quickly discovers there’s a new player in town. One who’s been around for thousands of years—and rode to war at the side of Kate’s father.<br /><br />This foe may be too much even for Kate and Curran, the Lord of the Beasts, to handle. Because this time, Kate will be taking on family…</span>

<span class="expandableContainer"><span class="truncatedContent">In the one I'm reading, Magic Bleeds, there is finally some Kate hanky-panky. It's not quite fade to black, but it's certainly not explicit, by my def<a class="jsShow showAction" href="#">…more</a></span><span class="fullContent">In the one I'm reading, Magic Bleeds, there is finally some Kate hanky-panky. It's not quite fade to black, but it's certainly not explicit, by my definition. Mostly, it's innuendo and inferences.<a class="jsHide hideAction" href="#">(less)</a></span></span>

    <a title="Katerina" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5014021-katerina"><img alt="Katerina" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1470667070p2/5014021.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1445814686?book_show_action=true">Nov 18, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Katerina" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Katerina" href="/user/show/5014021-katerina">Katerina</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5014021-katerina?shelf=paranormal">paranormal</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5014021-katerina?shelf=urban-fantasy">urban-fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5014021-katerina?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1445814686" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9488746996415790587"><u>Warning</u> <br/>The following review contains numerous crazy gifs and <b>incoherent fangirling</b>.Proceed with caution. <br/><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>“We had a fight,screamed at each other for a while,I kicked him in the head,and then he stayed the night.”</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1447930460ra/17069868.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/>I honestly tried to be calm.You know,cool,not overly excited.<s>After all,they're just fictional characters.</s>My ship has sailed,what's the big deal,right?I'm cool.<br/>So cool.<br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1440865798ra/16034394.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><b>MY SHIP HAS SAILED I DESERVE TO SCREAM AND SQUEAL AND DANCE AND HYPERVENTILATE AND FAINT AND ACT LIKE A CHILD</b></span>
  <span id="freeText9488746996415790587" style="display:none"><u>Warning</u> <br>The following review contains numerous crazy gifs and <b>incoherent fangirling</b>.Proceed with caution. <br><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>“We had a fight,screamed at each other for a while,I kicked him in the head,and then he stayed the night.”</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1447930460ra/17069868.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>I honestly tried to be calm.You know,cool,not overly excited.<s>After all,they're just fictional characters.</s>My ship has sailed,what's the big deal,right?I'm cool.<br>So cool.<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1440865798ra/16034394.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><b>MY SHIP HAS SAILED I DESERVE TO SCREAM AND SQUEAL AND DANCE AND HYPERVENTILATE AND FAINT AND ACT LIKE A CHILD THAT JUST MET SANTA!!!</b><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1382584829ra/6009401.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>*turns off fangirl mode*<br><br>Ok,I can continue now.<br><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>“Nothing good could possibly come from a plan that involved turning a man into a syphilis incubator.”</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br>Yeap that's right,after the flying palace and the rakshasas there is a new, more dangerous threat.The babylonian god of plague and chaos with seven deadly sidekicks decided to use Atlanta as a playground and eliminate competition by attacking the mighty forces of the city.Kate Daniels is the only one who can defeat this evil force,but the price is the revelation of her bloodline that might endanger everything she holds dear.<br><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>“The rabbis paled. I’d managed to terrify holy men. Maybe I could beat up a nun for an encore.” </blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br>After 3 books,one would expect that <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/21748.Ilona_Andrews" title="Ilona Andrews" rel="nofollow noopener">Ilona Andrews</a> would have trouble writing a compelling and fresh storyline,but that's far from the truth!<a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/6479550.Magic_Bleeds__Kate_Daniels___4_" title="Magic Bleeds (Kate Daniels, #4) by Ilona Andrews" rel="nofollow noopener">Magic Bleeds</a> combines <b>action,mystery and romance</b> wrapped up with <b>sarcasm</b> and <b>clever humor</b> and makes falling in love with the story and the characters inevitable!Reading the adventures of Kate Daniels and her furry friends is <b>effortless</b> and utterly <b>enjoyable</b>!I was once again sucked in a complex world full of <b>magic</b> and <b>blood</b> and I still crave more,more battles,more secrets,more sassiness,more ass-kicking,more Curran,<b>more everything</b>!<br><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>“He was mine.He cared for me,he made me lose all sense,he didn't give a damn about my father.He was what I wanted,because he made me happy.I wanted him like I'd never wanted anyone in my life.”</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br>Let me tell you this,the relationship between Kate and Curran was a crazy roller-coaster.Every single thing Kate felt,I felt it too.Anger,disappointment,betrayal,heartbreak,longing,happiness,love.She showed a more vulnerable side and I loved her even more for that.Kate and Curran are both arrogant assholes,and it took them some time to solve a terrible misunderstanding,but once they stopped behaving like children,Curran became Kate's own personal psycho and oh boy,it was good!<br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“You don't pick the family you're born into. You pick the one you make. I already chose my mate and glued her ass to the chair to make sure she knew it.” </i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1447714917ra/17040226.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>And OH MY GOD THEIR SCENES WERE <b>HOT HOT HOT HOT</b>!!!They never stopped fighting but that was sexy!!Curran is <b>the most delicious alpha-male ever</b>,but he could also be a romantic teddy bear that made me giggle and want to hug him!And do some other,<i>bad</i> things with him!<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1445234571ra/16619584.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>In case I didn't make myself clear,<b>I loved <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/6479550.Magic_Bleeds__Kate_Daniels___4_" title="Magic Bleeds (Kate Daniels, #4) by Ilona Andrews" rel="nofollow noopener">Magic Bleeds</a>!</b></span>
  <a data-text-id="9488746996415790587" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17232034458748555284">🐈 <b>The Adventures Of A Brave Little Kitty Buddy Rerererereread</b> (TAOABLKBR™) with the IA Addicts 🐈<br/><br/>➽ <b>
  <u>And the moral of this particular rererererereread is:</u>
</b> there's nothing quite like <b>magically delicious syphilis</b>, if you ask me.<br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1561279957ra/27712525.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>P.S.</b> Why the books in this series aren't <b>prescribed as antidepressants</b> is and forever will be one of the greatest mysteries of the universe. <br/><br/>👋 <b>Until next time and stuff</b>.<br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1479540926i/21203689._SX540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>[<b>January 2018</b>]<br/><br/>⚔ <b>
  <u>The Grand IAA™ KD Buddy Rerererereread Extravaganza</u>
</b> (GIAAKDBRE™), aka the <s>yellow bri</s></span>
  <span id="freeText17232034458748555284" style="display:none">🐈 <b>The Adventures Of A Brave Little Kitty Buddy Rerererereread</b> (TAOABLKBR™) with the IA Addicts 🐈<br><br>➽ <b>
  <u>And the moral of this particular rererererereread is:</u>
</b> there's nothing quite like <b>magically delicious syphilis</b>, if you ask me.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1561279957ra/27712525.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>P.S.</b> Why the books in this series aren't <b>prescribed as antidepressants</b> is and forever will be one of the greatest mysteries of the universe. <br><br>👋 <b>Until next time and stuff</b>.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1479540926i/21203689._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>[<b>January 2018</b>]<br><br>⚔ <b>
  <u>The Grand IAA™ KD Buddy Rerererereread Extravaganza</u>
</b> (GIAAKDBRE™), aka the <s>yellow brick</s> road to <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/17333180.Magic_Triumphs__Kate_Daniels___10_" title="Magic Triumphs (Kate Daniels, #10) by Ilona Andrews" rel="nofollow noopener">Magic Triumphs</a> ⚔<br><br><i><b>Presenting Episode 4</b>, or How Kate Daniels Learned Being Naught but a Little Squirrel Doesn't Mean You Can't Beat the Fish Out of the Deliciously Villainous Villains</i>.<br><br>➽ <b>
  <u>And the moral of this rererererererereread³ is</u>
</b>:<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1516186080i/24887721.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Also</b>, if you see <b>golden headlights</b> coming right at you while you're playing with your <b>deadly toothpick</b>, beware. Especially if there are <b>rolling tumble weeds</b> around. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1479540926i/21203689._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br> <br>[<b>June 2016</b>]<br> <br>❣ <b>KD is the Cure to All of Life's Problems Buddy Read</b> (KDitCtAoLPBR™) with my dear wife <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/4255477-angela" rel="nofollow noopener">Ange</a>, and the poor <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/group/show/148835-ilona-andrews-addicts-iaa" rel="nofollow noopener">IAA</a> souls who have fallen into our deathly <b>KD Surprise Reread Trap</b> (KSRT™).<br><br>· <b>Original rating</b>: 5 stars<br>· <b>Rating after xxxxxx rereads</b>: 100,000³ stars. More or less. Kate Daniels is IT. <b>Kate Daniels cannot be rated</b>.<br><br>» <b>And the moral of this particular rererereread is</b>: I want Ilona Andrews and <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/13026.Glen_Cook" title="Glen Cook" rel="nofollow noopener">Glen Cook</a> to <b>team up</b> and write a series/book/cereal box blurb/whatever/anything with Kate Daniels and <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/series/54284-the-chronicles-of-the-black-company" rel="nofollow noopener">Lady</a> as main characters. Now that would be <b>intergalactically EPIC</b>. And <b>epically INTERGALACTIC</b>. I'd read the story and never recover. Well maybe I would. If I rererererereread it over and over and over and over again. Forever after. And stuff. <b>It would be glorious</b>.<br><br>➽ <b>Ilona, Gordon, Glen</b>:<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1466696130i/19509457._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>The End</b> <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[until next time <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1479540926i/21203689._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>[Original review]<br><br><i>☆☆☆ Post-Shift Productions proudly present ☆☆☆</i><br><b>Yet Another Exciting Day in the Life of Kate Daniels</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1422176678i/13467151.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>►<b>8.00 a.m.:</b> investigate the death of a human barnacle. Realize it's a case of magically delicious syphilis. <b>It's going to be a long day</b>. Again.<br>► <b>8.30 a.m.:</b> think about His Furiness. <b>Feel like punching His Furiness in the face</b>. Where did that thought come from?<br>► <b>9.00 a.m.:</b> fight a demonic, spawn-of-hellish beast. <b>Good doggy</b>.<br>► <b>9.30 a.m.:</b> listen to your voice mail at work. <i>"I curse your arms so they will wither and die and fall off your body. <b>I curse your eyeballs to explode.</b> I curse your feet to swell until blue. I curse you. I curse you. I curse you."</i> <b>Okay then.</b><br>► <b>10.00 a.m.:</b> still investigating. A guy in a cloak did it. <b>Good to know</b>. Consider praying to Miss Marple.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1422346364i/13488602.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>► <b>10.30 a.m.:</b> find yourself doodling a <b>horned lion with a pie on his pitchfork</b>. Now who could that be?<br>► <b>11.00 a.m.:</b> trade your teenage werewolf sidekick for a <b>deadly, mutant attack poodle.</b><br>► <b>11.30 a.m.:</b> bubonic plague. Dysentery. Influenza. <b>Cholera on magic steroids.</b> What did you ever do to anybody? <br>► <b>12.00 a.m.:</b> wish that the furry bastard would stop intruding on your thoughts for five seconds. <b>Consider dancing a jig in celebration the minute it happens</b>.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1422346674i/13488642.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>► <b>12.30 a.m.:</b> discuss vamp storage cavities with Ghastek. <b>Find out he prefers throats to anuses.</b> Thank the gods for small favors.<br>► <b>1.00 p.m.:</b> friendly visit to the Mercenary Guild. Find a guy pinned to the elevator shaft by a spear through his throat. <b>Nifty.</b><br>► <b>1.30 p.m.:</b> Oh look, the Beast Lord. <i>Stay cool. Zen. <b>No punching in the face.</b> Punching would not be Zen.</i><br>► <b>2.00 p.m.:</b> be awed by His Fussiness' ability to use big words. A <s>friendly</s> conversation ensues. Consider throwing in some whistling. <b>And rolling thumbleweed.</b> You're all set. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1422214249ra/13472680.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>► <b>2.30 p.m.:</b> time for a well-deserved break. <b>Go home, resurrect a head in the kitchen</b>. Your deadly attack poodle barfs a little. <br>► <b>3.00 p.m.:</b> have His Furry Majesty throw you around a little. <b>Things are looking up.</b><br>► <b>3.30 p.m.:</b> get Raphael &amp; Andrea out of jail. Hot tub. SIG-Sauer P-226. <b>Diving for clams</b>. That's boudas for you.<br>► <b>4.00 p.m.:</b> sneak into the Keep. <b>Weld the bimbo room shut</b>. Decorate with catnip. Fun times. <br>► <b>4.30 p.m.:</b> go back to the office. Have a short phone conversation with His Furiness. <b>Realize your butt is glued to your chair. </b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1401709609ra/9836290.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>► <b>5.00 p.m.:</b> surprise visit from Auntie Erra. She came all the way from Babylon too. Coolest aunt ever. <b>This is one happy little squirrel.</b><br>► <b>5.30 p.m.:</b> Saiman suicidal. Curran homicidal. <b>Oh. My. God. The Universe just exploded. BIG TIME.</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1422182147ra/13468218.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>► <b>5.45 p.m.:</b> relax in a hot tub. Lose all sense. <i>
  <b>It's not the bathtub, baby.</b>
</i> Oh boy.<br>► <b>6.00 p.m.:</b> decide to give your <b>judgemental crocodile bodyguard</b> a room at the Keep. Think it might give Jim an aneurysm. <br>► <b>6.30 p.m.:</b> meet Auntie Erra again. Realize she recently developed a <b>fetish for spandex.</b> Why you?<br>► <b>7.00 p.m.:</b> bloodward. No problem. <b>Meow.</b> <br>► <b>7.30 p.m.:</b> pinned to the ground? No biggie. <b>Got a toothpick.</b><br>► <b>8.00 p.m.:</b> relax after a long day's work. <b>Read The Princess Bride</b> to a big sleeping cat.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1422344254ra/13488374.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>► <b>8.30 p.m.:</b> attend a lovely family reunion at the Keep. <b>Feel very welcome.</b> Challenge a few shapeshifters just for kicks. <br>► <b>9.00 p.m.:</b> read The Princess Bride to a big sleeping cat. Again. <b>Will this day never end?</b><br>► <b>9.30 p.m.:</b> meet a gay mongoose with an ambitious name. <b>Try to keep the creepy down a notch.</b> Fail miserably. <br>► <b>10.00 p.m.:</b> feline wake-up time. Attend yet another family reunion. <b>This is one pissed off little kitty</b>. RAWR. <b>Oh boy</b>. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1422119861i/13458929.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>· <b>Book 1</b>: <a   <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1104210540" />
    <a title="Rachel Reads Ravenously" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/14514998-rachel-reads-ravenously"><img alt="Rachel Reads Ravenously" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1539149211p2/14514998.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1104210540?book_show_action=true">Nov 12, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Rachel Reads Ravenously" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Rachel Reads Ravenously" href="/user/show/14514998-rachel-reads-ravenously">Rachel Reads Ravenously</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14514998-rachel-reads-ravenously?shelf=fantasy">fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14514998-rachel-reads-ravenously?shelf=urban-fantasy">urban-fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14514998-rachel-reads-ravenously?shelf=werewolves-shapeshifters">werewolves-shapeshifters</a>,

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14514998-rachel-reads-ravenously?shelf=paranormal-romance">paranormal-romance</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1104210540" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16896949250690213368"><i> Reread 7/2018 </i><br/><br/><b> 4.5 stars! </b><br/><br/><b> <i> “I can't give you the white picket fence, and if I did, you'd set it on fire.” </i> </b><br/><br/><a href='http://s177.photobucket.com/user/dawnygirl07/media/magicbleedscollage.png.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1415945546i/11868317.png' alt=' photo magicbleedscollage.png' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>I'm a giant fan of urban fantasy. I read all kinds of genres of books, but when I read urban fantasy I get a feeling of being at home. The Ilona Andrews writing team created a universe where when I'm having a bad day or want to have a good time, I can open a paperback, and escape there effortlessly and happily. And that's exactly what I did with this book. I recently had some crap com</span>
  <span id="freeText16896949250690213368" style="display:none"><i> Reread 7/2018 </i><br><br><b> 4.5 stars! </b><br><br><b> <i> “I can't give you the white picket fence, and if I did, you'd set it on fire.” </i> </b><br><br><a href="http://s177.photobucket.com/user/dawnygirl07/media/magicbleedscollage.png.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1415945546i/11868317.png" alt=" photo magicbleedscollage.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>I'm a giant fan of urban fantasy. I read all kinds of genres of books, but when I read urban fantasy I get a feeling of being at home. The Ilona Andrews writing team created a universe where when I'm having a bad day or want to have a good time, I can open a paperback, and escape there effortlessly and happily. And that's exactly what I did with this book. I recently had some crap come up in my personal life, and when I had the chance I transported myself into this world of mercenaries and werebeasts and didn't want to come back out. So massive kudos to the authors, you did your job right.<br><br>In magic flare zone Atlanta, Kate Daniels is stood up. That's right, she cooked the Beast Lord Curran dinner, and he never showed. Flash forward about a month or so and the two are at each others' throats. On top of this, there's a strange shaman who keeps showing up in bars and casinos and trying to magic blast the place with plague and disease. It's not long before Kate gets called onto the case, and when she does she finds she might be more connected to it than she expected.<br><br>This was the best book of this series for me so far. The plot was thrilling, the banter was witty and humorous, and I couldn't put the darn book down even when my eyelids were slowly closing due to a need for sleep. <br><br>My favorite part of the book? The pranks Kate and Curran were playing on each other. When she covered his bed in catnip and he glued her ass to her office chair? Priceless. The addition of the attack poodle to Kate's daily life only made the story more entertaining.<br><br><b> <i> "....I think a dog is a great idea. I just never pictured you with a mutant poodle.” <br>“He isn’t a poodle. He’s a Doberman mix."<br>“Aha. Keep telling yourself that.” </i> </b><br><br>Also, another reason why this book was awesome? It's the hook up book! Yes, the Kate and Curran relationship finally comes to a explosive collision in this book and it was all it was cracked up to be.<br><br><b> <i> "I miss you. I worry about you. I worry something stupid will happen and I won't be there and you'll be gone. I worry we won't ever get a chance and it's driving me out of my skull." </i> </b> <br><br>This was also the book where I finally stopped skimming when it came to the plot. By this I mean the underlying issue or mystery. As much as I love the other books and their stories, there were points when I skimmed. That didn't really happen in this book. All of Kate's investigations had me utterly enthralled, and the parts with Kate and Erra was like watching an interrogation between a smart ass and a sociopath (it would make great television, just saying).<br><br>And that ending? <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ When they finally got to flip it and Kate took care of Curran when he was injured? Heartwarming. It gave the viewer a small glimpse of what Curran goes through when Kate was injured or sick.  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br><br> <b> <i> "You don't pick the family you're born into. You pick the one you make. I already chose my mate and glued her ass to the chair to make sure she knew it.” </i> </b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1494101706i/22685352._SX540_.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Follow me on ♥ <a href="http://www.facebook.com/rachelreadsravenously" rel="nofollow noopener">Facebook</a> ♥ <a href="http://rachelsreadsravenously.com" rel="nofollow noopener">Blog</a> ♥ <a href="http://instagram.com/rachelreadsravenously" rel="nofollow noopener">Instagram</a> ♥ <a href="https://twitter.com/rayliz89" rel="nofollow noopener">Twitter</a> ♥<br></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>
  <a data-text-id="16896949250690213368" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Tadiana ✩Night Owl☽" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Tadiana ✩Night Owl☽" href="/user/show/8734459-tadiana-night-owl">Tadiana ✩Night Owl☽</a>

        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8734459-tadiana-night-owl?shelf=urban-fantasy">urban-fantasy</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1254890894" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14395109592842811014">4.33 stars. While <i>Magic Bleeds</i> doesn't quite hit the heights of the third book, <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/4345498.Magic_Strikes__Kate_Daniels___3_' title='Magic Strikes (Kate Daniels, #3) by Ilona Andrews' rel='nofollow noopener'>Magic Strikes</a>, it's still a great, action-packed book.<br/><br/>As a mercenary peacekeeper, Kate gets called to investigate a strangely intense fight at a bar. When she gets there, there's a body strung up on a utility pole, pinned to it with a crowbar. The body is very dead ... but the deadly disease that infests him is NOT. As magically virulent flesh-colored fuzz starts creeping toward Kate and others, it's all Kate can do </span>
  <span id="freeText14395109592842811014" style="display:none">4.33 stars. While <i>Magic Bleeds</i> doesn't quite hit the heights of the third book, <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/4345498.Magic_Strikes__Kate_Daniels___3_" title="Magic Strikes (Kate Daniels, #3) by Ilona Andrews" rel="nofollow noopener">Magic Strikes</a>, it's still a great, action-packed book.<br /><br />As a mercenary peacekeeper, Kate gets called to investigate a strangely intense fight at a bar. When she gets there, there's a body strung up on a utility pole, pinned to it with a crowbar. The body is very dead ... but the deadly disease that infests him is NOT. As magically virulent flesh-colored fuzz starts creeping toward Kate and others, it's all Kate can do to try to contain it within magical ward circles.<br /><br />This is just the start of troubles for Kate. Two more attacks occur, more dead bodies pile up, more magically mobile diseases attack. As it turns out, someone with a very long relationship (think centuries, even millennia) with Kate's magical father has Kate, the Pack, and Atlanta generally in their sights.<br /><br />Meanwhile, after things had started looking up for Kate's slow-developing relationship with Curran the Beast Lord at the end of book #3, it all comes crashing down at the beginning of this one: Curran doesn't show up for an EXTREMELY significant dinner for two, with no explanation, and Kate gets blown off when she calls the Keep (the shapeshifter's Atlanta compound) to check on him. Being Kate, she doesn't take it at all well. The question is, who can out-stubborn who? <br /><br /><i>Magic Bleeds</i> is a solid entry in the Kate Daniels urban fantasy series, with the familiar mixture of vampires, werewolves and other shapechangers, ancient and exotic gods (this type we're dealing with Babylonian legends), sometimes unreliable magic, and a major helping of snark. This one is noteworthy for some serious changes in Kate's life and some significant revelations about her past and her ancestry.<br /><br />You know those books that keep you up way too late at night because you just need to finish them since you just can't leave the characters hanging where they are? Yeah, this is one of those. And the second time I read it, instead of staying up all hours, I read it during the day while I should've been doing other things. But Curran and Kate kept calling to me ...</span>
  <a data-text-id="14395109592842811014" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jessica ❁ ➳ Silverbow ➳ ❁ " class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jessica ❁ ➳ Silverbow ➳ ❁ " href="/user/show/10336538-jessica-silverbow">Jessica ❁ ➳ Silverbow ➳ ❁ </a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer351592946" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11357273762559945937"><b>9/30/17 - ON SALE for $2.99:</b><br/><br/><a href='http://www.amazon.com/gp/product/B003NX7NHO/ref=as_li_ss_il?ie=UTF8&camp=1789&creative=390957&creativeASIN=B003NX7NHO&linkCode=as2&tag=rabrea-20' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1506700748i/24044234.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1506700748i/24044235.gif' width='1' height='1' alt='' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><a target='_blank' rel='noopener nofollow' href='http://amzn.to/2xLJQ5t'>http://amzn.to/2xLJQ5t</a><br/><br/>Geez, friggin', Louise . . . <br/><br/>Just in case you've somehow missed my enthusiasm for Kate #3, MAGIC STRIKES, I'll say (at least) one more time that it is my favorite installment in a UF series ever. <br/><br/>And it is. <br/><br/>But MAGIC BLEEDS gets 5 stars too. <br/><br/>It's maybe my second favorite installment in a Urban Fantasy series ever. It's been too long since I've read BITTEN by Kelley Armstrong (best first installment in an UF series ever), to say for sure . . .</span>
  <span id="freeText11357273762559945937" style="display:none"><b>9/30/17 - ON SALE for $2.99:</b><br><br><a href="http://www.amazon.com/gp/product/B003NX7NHO/ref=as_li_ss_il?ie=UTF8&amp;camp=1789&amp;creative=390957&amp;creativeASIN=B003NX7NHO&amp;linkCode=as2&amp;tag=rabrea-20" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1506700748i/24044234.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1506700748i/24044235.gif" width="1" height="1" alt="" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://amzn.to/2xLJQ5t">http://amzn.to/2xLJQ5t</a><br><br>Geez, friggin', Louise . . . <br><br>Just in case you've somehow missed my enthusiasm for Kate #3, MAGIC STRIKES, I'll say (at least) one more time that it is my favorite installment in a UF series ever. <br><br>And it is. <br><br>But MAGIC BLEEDS gets 5 stars too. <br><br>It's maybe my second favorite installment in a Urban Fantasy series ever. It's been too long since I've read BITTEN by Kelley Armstrong (best first installment in an UF series ever), to say for sure . . . but it's a close thing, either way.<br><br>And I love MAGIC STRIKES and MAGIC BLEEDS for similar, yet very different reasons.<br><br>One of my favorite (and simultaneously least favorite) things about blogging is that it's made me think about <i>why </i>I like or dislike something in a book. Sometimes I miss the simplicity of finishing a book, saying, "I love it, it RAWKED," then moving on to the next thing, but on the whole, I think I get more out of the books I read now.<br><br>For example, this is probably the fifth time I've read Kate #4, but it's the first time I've realized that the more one of these books touches on her family history, the more I like it. Same goes for how direct the link between the Bad Guy and that history (Roland) is. <br><br>In book 3, the Bad Guys were Roland's flunkies.<br><br>In MAGIC BLEEDS . . . well, I can't tell you who the Bad Guy is, but suffice it to say, NOT a flunkie. And for those of you (like me) who devour every, single speck of Kate lore, you will be so ridiculously happy with this book. Just after the mid-way point, is History of Roland 101. Back to Bad Guy though, this one is both enthralling and terrifying. Bad Guy is crazy. No, really. Total psychopath. But at the same time Bad Guy is . . . "<i>ruthlessly intelligent</i>." <br><br><blockquote>
  <i>"Why call them half-breeds?"<br>"It's a convenient term. It drips with contempt. Your're a soldier who faces a monstrosity. It's stronger and faster than you, it looks like a nightmare, and when it takes a wound that would kill a normal man, its fellows push you back and fifteen minutes later the creature you wounded is back on its feet. Where will your courage come from?"<br>I leaned toward her. "But if you think the creature is an abomination, a half-breed, who is less than you, you might reach deep inside and find a pair..."<br>"Exactly."</i>
</blockquote><br>MAGIC BLEEDS is full of these insightful, little life lessons, and for the first time, you begin to understand what Kate is up against. Her enemy is THOUSANDS of years old, with THOUSANDS of years worth of not just knowledge, but <i>application</i> of that knowledge.<br><br><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[I think the Andrews are particularly clever here when they make Kate an almost mirror image of her aunt. It lends credulity to Kate living through the inevitable showdown with Roland--yes, Kate is infinitely less experienced, but as Erra said, "<i>Blood ran true</i>," and Kate has proven on numerous occasions that she is adaptable and quick on her feet. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br>Seriously fantastic villain and history lesson aside, there are a multitude of other reasons to love this book. Most of those reasons can be boiled down to Kate being Kate and Curran being Curran. It's not a spoiler to tell you that Curran doesn't show for the naked dinner, b/c it's the very first thing that happens in this book. Now imagine all the various ways that could play out, and you start to get an idea of the epic awesomeness of this book. <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[There is nothing better than an affectionate Curran . . . except for maybe a throwing-you-on-the-floor-to-have-his-way-with-you Curran. But hey, LUCKY you, you don't have to decide, you get them BOTH. Oh yeaaah. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> YEP. It's that good. LOVE it.<br><br><b>My other reviews for this series:</b><br><br><b>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer723399178" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11248185042767944274"><b>Sale Alert:</b> Books 3 and 4 of this series were my absolute favorites which is saying something since this is one of my all time favorite UF series. This book is currently on sale 9/30/17 <a href='https://www.amazon.com/gp/product/B003NX7NHO/ref=series_rw_dp_sw' rel='nofollow noopener'>$1.99</a><br/><br/>Yes I'm reading the Kate Daniels Series AGAIN and guess what I love it a little more every time. 3rd read and this series is still so much fun and at the top of my short list for UF/PRN. Kate/Curran and Saiman have all the best parts in this.<br/><br/>Buddy Read/Reread June 8 with the gang at <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/group/show/148835-ilona-andrews-addicts-iaa' rel='nofollow noopener'>Ilona Andrews Addicts (IA</a></span>
  <span id="freeText11248185042767944274" style="display:none"><b>Sale Alert:</b> Books 3 and 4 of this series were my absolute favorites which is saying something since this is one of my all time favorite UF series. This book is currently on sale 9/30/17 <a href="https://www.amazon.com/gp/product/B003NX7NHO/ref=series_rw_dp_sw" rel="nofollow noopener">$1.99</a><br><br>Yes I'm reading the Kate Daniels Series AGAIN and guess what I love it a little more every time. 3rd read and this series is still so much fun and at the top of my short list for UF/PRN. Kate/Curran and Saiman have all the best parts in this.<br><br>Buddy Read/Reread June 8 with the gang at <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/group/show/148835-ilona-andrews-addicts-iaa" rel="nofollow noopener">Ilona Andrews Addicts (IAA)</a><br><br><br><b>Re-read...YAY I'm finally to my favorite book in the series for my re-read before Magic Breaks<br><br>Review after Re-read 7/15/14</b><br><br><a href="http://s1267.photobucket.com/user/FionaFixit/media/highsix_zpsab9390d3.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1405358990ra/10386146.gif" alt=" photo highsix_zpsab9390d3.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>This was my favorite in the series the first time through and I believe it safely retains that ranking this time as well. In my first read through I remember hurrying through parts to get to what was going to happen between Kate and Curran. This time I have the luxury of knowing what will become of them so I was able to focus on all the other great stuff happening as well.<br><br>Some of the best parts are the great side characters. The introduction of Kate’s new best friend with four legs that looks like a mutant attack poodle was so much fun. I love animal companions in novels.<br><a href="http://s1267.photobucket.com/user/FionaFixit/media/ClickHandlerashx_zps562d4e9b.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1405358991i/10386147.jpg" alt=" photo ClickHandlerashx_zps562d4e9b.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><b>
  <i>“You should name him Fezzik,” Andrea said. <br>“Inconceivable,” I told her and took the canine traitor back to my office.</i>
</b><br><br>Alas the dog’s name does not end up being Fezzik but it is much cooler and l loved the reason Kate choose it for him. Once again proving our girl has brains and brawn.<br><br>But my absolute favorite side character in this is Aunt B. I loved her the first time through as well but this time I really could appreciate just how smart and crafty that lady is. Nothing gets past her and she does seem to have Kate’s best interest at heart especially if it helps out the Bouda clan as well.<br><a href="http://s1267.photobucket.com/user/FionaFixit/media/auntbashx_zps07453e32.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1405358991i/10386148.jpg" alt=" photo auntbashx_zps07453e32.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b><i>”Did he spend the night?”<br>Putting claws to my throat was never a good idea. I smiled. “None of your business.”<br>“So he did. Did he use the word ‘mate’?”<br>“What happened between me and Curran is our own affair.”<br>Aunt B raised her eyebrows. “Congratulations. Then you are indeed, the mate.”<br>Why me? “That would be news to me.”<br>“I wouldn’t be surprised if you were the last to know.”</i> </b><br><br>Saiman, I forgot how wonderfully charming that man/quarter god could be when he wants to be. He has some fantastic interactions with Kate and while he might have overestimated his position in a few things I love some of the scenes with him, especially when he was pulling on deaths whiskers this time around.<br><br>KATE AND CURRAN!!! Yes this is the book they finally get down to the nitty gritty. It isn’t all roses and sunshine they are both alpha material and totally clash while trying to maintain their dominance. But my girl Kate once she decides what she wants she is ALL IN and nothing and no one will separate her from His Furriness.<br><br><b>
  <i>“If you come, you better come in force because I will kill every single one of you. My hand won't shake, my aim won't falter. My face will be the last thing you'll see before you die." I jammed my knife into the table and walked out.”</i>
</b><br><br><a href="http://photobucket.com/images/easy%20a" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1405358991i/10386149.jpg" alt="easy a photo: Easy a 55419670-1321846626-Easy-a-4.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Forward ho onto the next great installment of the series.<br><br>If you are a fan of UF/PRN at all this is a fantastically fun series……<b>READ IT!!!</b><br><br><br><b>Original Review 9/28/13</b><br><br>Before I totally fangirl over the Kate/Curran drama …oh and I totally will….I’ll attempt to talk about the rest of the book.<br><br>One of the things I like about the Kate Daniels series is that the villain is always based in some sort of lore that I haven’t been overexposed to I’m not even sure if it is real or just made up. In that I feel like I’m learning a little bit more but also I don’t already have a bunch of preconceived notions of how the god/mythical creature should act and it is like starting with a clean sheet.<br><br>The villain in this installment is undoubtedly the most dangerous and complex that Kate has faced to date. The bad guy carries seven plagues around with them and unleashes them at different times on Atlanta. Each one is devastating and causes incredible havoc. They also have some strange similarities in power to Kate and she doesn’t know how to control her power nearly as well and needs to learn fast.<br>Hugh is busy gathering information on Kate to make sure he knows everything about her before presenting her to Roland and is biding his time through this newest crisis. Kate knows that soon she will have to face her father and is desperately struggling with either going it completely alone or letting people into her life. But to do that she will have to come clean and tell the people closest to her who she really is.<br><br><b>
  <i>You can’t smelt happiness out of a lie. The world doesn’t work that way.</i>
</b><br><br>The character I most enjoyed this book beside the new addition of the attack poodle and Kate and Curran or course was Aunt B. She is sneaky, manipulative, intelligent an opportunist and at times even the voice of reason. I really like the way she runs her clan of hyenas and how she interacts with Kate. Aunt B is the alpha that you definitely do not want to get on the wrong side of. The deal she makes with Kate is one that benefits Kate but also helps her. I like how she is an example and a strong female character without being portrayed exclusively as a bitch. <br><br>The plot arc was one of the strongest of the series and delved into the magic of the world Kate lives in even more. This is probably the strongest book in the series to date. <br><br>Okay on to the fangirling of the romance aspect of this book. There may be a few minor spoilers don’t read on if you don’t want to know.<br><br>Cat courting practices are interesting to say the least and a little dangerous it seems to any that stand to close…ehmm Saiman cough cough. I was worried at the beginning of the story that the minor misunderstanding between Kate and Curran was going to derail them for an entire book (I’ve seen it done in other series and I’m not a fan) but no worries all is made well again before the end.<br>Kate miserable without Curran in her life decides to try to play by his rules and it is about time. I loved that she finally decided, this is what I want, and took charge. Even if later she doubts herself and her choices I admire the initial push in the right direction. <br><br>There are some very good steamy scenes and I love that everything isn’t roses for them right after. They have distinctly different personalities and wants. Curran is desperate to protect Kate and Kate is desperate to run into the face of danger and sacrifice herself if needed. But tenderness and vulnerability are definitely there at the blooming of their relationship.<br><br><b>
  <i>“People think I built the Pack, because I'm the guy who has the welfare of all shapeshifters in mind. They're wrong. Everything I built, I did so that when I mate and have children, nobody can touch my family. (...) I built all this so I can protect you.”</i>
</b><br><br>Plus being Mated to the Beast Lord isn’t all glamorous. You live in a glass house always surrounded by people watching looking for an edge something to give them the upper hand looking for any weakness to exploit. I couldn’t believe how fast some of the pack turned after the main battle. <br><br>I’m ecstatic that Kate and Curran have finally made some progress on this front since the tension between them was killing me. Like the end of other books in this series it really just made me want more. I can’t wait to see what will happen to the main Alpha’s next.</span>

<span id="freeTextContainer5671304988811472410"><b>First reread January 2015<br/><br/>Original rating: 5<br/>New rating: 8</b><br/><br/><i>☆☆☆ Post-Shift Productions proudly present ☆☆☆</i><br/><b>Yet Another Exciting Day in the Life of Kate Daniels</b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1422176678i/13467151.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>►<b>8.00 a.m.:</b> investigate the death of a human barnacle. Realize it's a case of magically delicious syphilis. <b>It's going to be a long day</b>. Again.<br/>► <b>8.30 a.m.:</b> think about His Furiness. <b>Feel like punching His Furiness in the face</b>. Where did that thought come from?<br/>► <b>9.00 a.m.:</b> fight a demonic, spawn-of-hellish beast. <b>Good doggy</b>.<br/>► <b>9.30 a.m.:</b> listen t</span>
  <span id="freeText5671304988811472410" style="display:none"><b>First reread January 2015<br><br>Original rating: 5<br>New rating: 8</b><br><br><i>☆☆☆ Post-Shift Productions proudly present ☆☆☆</i><br><b>Yet Another Exciting Day in the Life of Kate Daniels</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1422176678i/13467151.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>►<b>8.00 a.m.:</b> investigate the death of a human barnacle. Realize it's a case of magically delicious syphilis. <b>It's going to be a long day</b>. Again.<br>► <b>8.30 a.m.:</b> think about His Furiness. <b>Feel like punching His Furiness in the face</b>. Where did that thought come from?<br>► <b>9.00 a.m.:</b> fight a demonic, spawn-of-hellish beast. <b>Good doggy</b>.<br>► <b>9.30 a.m.:</b> listen to your voice mail at work. <i>"I curse your arms so they will wither and die and fall off your body. <b>I curse your eyeballs to explode.</b> I curse your feet to swell until blue. I curse you. I curse you. I curse you."</i> <b>Okay then.</b><br>► <b>10.00 a.m.:</b> still investigating. A guy in a cloak did it. <b>Good to know</b>. Consider praying to Miss Marple.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1422346364i/13488602.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>► <b>10.30 a.m.:</b> find yourself doodling a <b>horned lion with a pie on his pitchfork</b>. Now who could that be?<br>► <b>11.00 a.m.:</b> trade your teenage werewolf sidekick for a <b>deadly, mutant attack poodle.</b><br>► <b>11.30 a.m.:</b> bubonic plague. Dysentery. Influenza. <b>Cholera on magic steroids.</b> What did you ever do to anybody? <br>► <b>12.00 a.m.:</b> wish that the furry bastard would stop intruding on your thoughts for five seconds. <b>Consider dancing a jig in celebration the minute it happens</b>.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1422346674i/13488642.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>► <b>12.30 a.m.:</b> discuss vamp storage cavities with Ghastek. <b>Find out he prefers throats to anuses.</b> Thank the gods for small favors.<br>► <b>1.00 p.m.:</b> friendly visit to the Mercenary Guild. Find a guy pinned to the elevator shaft by a spear through his throat. <b>Nifty.</b><br>► <b>1.30 p.m.:</b> Oh look, the Beast Lord. <i>Stay cool. Zen. <b>No punching in the face.</b> Punching would not be Zen.</i><br>► <b>2.00 p.m.:</b> be awed by His Fussiness' ability to use big words. A <s>friendly</s> conversation ensues. Consider throwing in some whistling. <b>And rolling thumbleweed.</b> You're all set. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1422214249ra/13472680.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>► <b>2.30 p.m.:</b> time for a well-deserved break. <b>Go home, resurrect a head in the kitchen</b>. Your deadly attack poodle barfs a little. <br>► <b>3.00 p.m.:</b> have His Furry Majesty throw you around a little. <b>Things are looking up.</b><br>► <b>3.30 p.m.:</b> get Raphael &amp; Andrea out of jail. Hot tub. SIG-Sauer P-226. <b>Diving for clams</b>. That's boudas for you.<br>► <b>4.00 p.m.:</b> sneak into the Keep. <b>Weld the bimbo room shut</b>. Decorate with catnip. Fun times. <br>► <b>4.30 p.m.:</b> go back to the office. Have a short phone conversation with His Furiness. <b>Realize your butt is glued to your chair. </b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1401709609ra/9836290.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>► <b>5.00 p.m.:</b> surprise visit from Auntie Erra. She came all the way from Babylon too. Coolest aunt ever. <b>This is one happy little squirrel.</b><br>► <b>5.30 p.m.:</b> Saiman suicidal. Curran homicidal. <b>Oh. My. God. The Universe just exploded. BIG TIME.</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1422182147ra/13468218.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>► <b>5.45 p.m.:</b> relax in a hot tub. Lose all sense. <i>
  <b>It's not the bathtub, baby.</b>
</i> Oh boy.<br>► <b>6.00 p.m.:</b> decide to give your <b>judgemental crocodile bodyguard</b> a room at the Keep. Think it might give Jim an aneurysm. <br>► <b>6.30 p.m.:</b> meet Auntie Erra again. Realize she recently developed a <b>fetish for spandex.</b> Why you?<br>► <b>7.00 p.m.:</b> bloodward. No problem. <b>Meow.</b> <br>► <b>7.30 p.m.:</b> pinned to the ground? No biggie. <b>Got a toothpick.</b><br>► <b>8.00 p.m.:</b> relax after a long day's work. <b>Read The Princess Bride</b> to a big sleeping cat.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1422344254ra/13488374.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>► <b>8.30 p.m.:</b> attend a lovely family reunion at the Keep. <b>Feel very welcome.</b> Challenge a few shapeshifters just for kicks. <br>► <b>9.00 p.m.:</b> read The Princess Bride to a big sleeping cat. Again. <b>Will this day never end?</b><br>► <b>9.30 p.m.:</b> meet a gay mongoose with an ambitious name. <b>Try to keep the creepy down a notch.</b> Fail miserably. <br>► <b>10.00 p.m.:</b> feline wake-up time. Attend yet another family reunion. <b>This is one pissed off little kitty</b>. RAWR. <b>Oh boy</b>.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1422119861i/13458929.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br> <br>**********<br><b>Original review (June 2014):</b><br><br><b>This series is killing me!</b> How much sleep do I have to lose over it?? Magic Bleeds is such an amazing read that by the time I finished the book I wasn’t sure whether I wanted to read it again or jump right to the next one…<blockquote>
<b>I could do this.</b> I just had to stay cool. Zen. No punching in the face. <b>Punching would not be Zen.</b>
</blockquote><b>Well, to be honest,</b> the first part of the book wasn’t that fantastic but the second half simply blew me away. Why? Action, mystery, the usual Kate badassery, lots of emotion, some downright heart-breaking moments and humour, lots of it.<blockquote>
<b>A lion roar burst through the phone.</b> I held it away from my ear until he was done. “Very scary. I feel it’s my duty to remind you that threatening a member of law enforcement is punishable by law. If you would like to file a petition regarding your break-in, the Order will gladly look into the matter for you.” The phone fell silent. <b>Oh God, I gave him an aneurysm.</b>
</blockquote><b>In this instalment we get more details</b> about Kate’s blood and lineage (lovely family!) and learn about the Pack rules &amp; regulations in detail (such complexity, I love that!). Kate becoming Curran’s mate is wreaking havoc in the Pack politics, with most of its members suffering from a <b>collective panic attack</b>. This new situation is unsettling for most of the weres and gives a new edge to the series, with some unexpected twists &amp; developments.<blockquote>
  <b>Kate Daniels, deadly swordmaster. Fear my twitching pinkie.</b>
</blockquote><b>Kate.</b> Do I really have to go into this? Okay. Hall Hail the Queen of Snarky Badasses. <b>I rest my case.</b><blockquote>
<b>The rabbis paled.</b> I’d managed to terrify holy men. <b>Maybe I could beat up a nun for an encore.</b>
</blockquote><b>The Kate/Curran love story</b> does take precedence over the action in this instalment, which apparently disappointed some readers. I actually liked that the romance part of the series was only a subplot until now and was afraid this would turn into some boring paranormal romance thing. Well, fear not for Ilona Andrews handles things very well. <b>I was annoyed at first</b> because Kate &amp; Curran were both acting stubborn and very childish but it didn’t last long. Besides, things never get corny-mushy between them. With these two? Oh no. <b>They’d rather rip each other apart first!</b> This is no bunnies &amp; rainbows romance. We get some very serious conversations between Kate &amp; His Fuzziness but mostly we get hilarious scenes. The mating game is just hilarious. <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Kate shutting Curran out of the slut hut! Curran gluing Kate's butt to her chair! <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> It doesn’t get much better than that!<blockquote>
<b>“What’s this?”</b><br>“A needle.”<br>“What should I do with it?” He’d walked right into it. Too easy.<br><b>“Please use it to pop your head. It’s obscuring my view of the room.”</b>
</blockquote><b>Yes. I'm in love with this series.</b> Yes. I want to be Kate Daniels when I grow up. <b>Yes I need to get my hands on the next instalment NOW.</b><br><br>• <b>Book 1</b>: <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1156913295" rel="nofollow noopener">Magic Bites</a> ★★★★★<br>• <b>Book 2</b>: <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1136556683" rel="nofollow noopener">Magic Burns</a> ★★★★★<br>• <b>Book 3</b>: <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1222658742" rel="nofollow noopener">Magic Strikes</a> ★★★★★<br>• <b>Book 5</b>: <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1156907200" rel="nofollow noopener">Magic Slays</a> ★★★★★<br>• <b>Book 6</b>: <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1087380222" rel="nofollow noopener">Magic Rises</a> ★★★★★<br>• <b>Book 7</b>: <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1222671908" rel="nofollow noopener">Magic Breaks</a> ★★★★★<br>• <b>Book 8</b>: <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1088122695" rel="nofollow noopener">Magic Shifts</a> ★★★★★<br>• <b>Book 9</b>: <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1388386563" rel="nofollow noopener">Magic Binds</a> ★★★★★<br>• <b>Book 10</b>: <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1767301739" rel="nofollow noopener">Magic Triumphs</a> ★★★★</["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

Shapeshifters going mad to town on the verge of epidemic, add Kate's dark mood over Curran standing her up for the dinner to the mix; it was a rollercoaster ride. So many moments where I laughed out loud, and bit my nails (specially those final battle scenes). An enjoyable read. </span>

<div id="review_1796678230" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1796678230" />
    <a title="Sophia Triad" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/44642860-sophia-triad"><img alt="Sophia Triad" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1591419108p2/44642860.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1796678230?book_show_action=true">Oct 28, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Sophia Triad" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Sophia Triad" href="/user/show/44642860-sophia-triad">Sophia Triad</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/44642860-sophia-triad?shelf=lions">lions</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/44642860-sophia-triad?shelf=1paranormal-lovestories">1paranormal-lovestories</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/44642860-sophia-triad?shelf=witches-wizards">witches-wizards</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/44642860-sophia-triad?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/44642860-sophia-triad?shelf=shifters">shifters</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/44642860-sophia-triad?shelf=vampires">vampires</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/44642860-sophia-triad?shelf=wolves-lycans">wolves-lycans</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1796678230" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9742555972594483640">Allow me to tell you about Kate’s family:<br/><br/>HER FAMILY FROM THE PAST:<br/>1. Her biological father, Roland. We finally learn the true story of Roland, the story of his first children and the first vampire he had created. Kate tells the story to a golem to emphasize the power of the blood that runs in her veins.<br/>2. Her mother. We learn how she feels about her mother and her importance. Kate shows an old picture of her to Andrea. Unfortunately Kate has no memories and no recollection of her mother and her </span>
  <span id="freeText9742555972594483640" style="display:none">Allow me to tell you about Kate’s family:<br /><br />HER FAMILY FROM THE PAST:<br />1. Her biological father, Roland. We finally learn the true story of Roland, the story of his first children and the first vampire he had created. Kate tells the story to a golem to emphasize the power of the blood that runs in her veins.<br />2. Her mother. We learn how she feels about her mother and her importance. Kate shows an old picture of her to Andrea. Unfortunately Kate has no memories and no recollection of her mother and her step father being together.<br />3. Her aunt and her seven undead servants. Kate and her bloodthirsty auntie have a “pleasant reunion”. They share memories and stories. They have a cup of tea. Her aunt talks about her old goldfishes, about the loved ones who come and go through the centuries. She talks about how badly she would like to destroy Atlanta and kill every available shapeshifter. They fight to death.<br /><br />HER FAMILY FROM THE PRESENT:<br />1. Her best friend Andrea. The closet beastkin hyena is in trouble and Kate does not hesitate to offer a real valuable artifact to get her and her boyfriend, Raphael, off the hook. Kate will not hesitate to help Andrea at any cost and any time. <br />2. Her adopted niece, Julie. Kate agonizes for her safety. She is crazy of worry in case something happens to Julie. She is afraid that her psychopath aunt will try to hurt Julie in order to hurt Kate.<br />3. The Pack. They have become her closest friends. They run to her rescue, they patch her injuries, they make her feel safe. They are her true home. Kate will not let anyone think less of them and call them nonhuman.<br />4. The dog. Kate unexpectedly is the proud owner of a poodle who loves to vomit and bark to creatures that threaten Kate. Kate will have a hard time finding a name for him. Everything else will come easy.<br />5. Greg’s House. Maybe it is time for Kate to say her goodbyes and move on. The Keep is waiting for her.<br /><br />HER FUTURE FAMILY:<br />Obviously.<br />Curran. Curran. Curran. Curran.<br />The disappointing dinner date will be a good start for Kate to acknowledge her feelings for Curran.<br />The silent treatment, after the disappointing dinner date, will be a good start for Curran to acknowledge the sacrifices he is willing to make for Kate.<br />The games they play and the hilarious pranks they pull on each other, after the explanations about the disappointing dinner date, will make the start of their mating easier. <br />The games and the pranks will be definitely a pure delight for readers as well.<br /><br />Well this is one these books. These books you want to start reading again, the second you finish them. <br />The best book so far in the series. I absolutely loved it! </span>
  <a data-text-id="9742555972594483640" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_1056391157" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1056391157" />
    <a title="Evgeny" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/9340136-evgeny"><img alt="Evgeny" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1544797852p2/9340136.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1056391157?book_show_action=true">Sep 16, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Evgeny" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Evgeny" href="/user/show/9340136-evgeny">Evgeny</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9340136-evgeny?shelf=fantasy">fantasy</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1056391157" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5908862496319312852">Buddy read with <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/5600230-armina' rel='nofollow noopener'>Armina</a>, <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/17237503-eilonwy' rel='nofollow noopener'>Eilonwy</a>, <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/3328287-asya' rel='nofollow noopener'>Asya</a>, and <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/22911953-monty-cupcake' rel='nofollow noopener'>Monty Cupcake</a>.<br/><br/>Kate Daniels, an expert swordswoman works for the Order of Knights - an organization which solves magic problems. Kate does her solving part by chopping the given problem into small pieces with her sword appropriately called Slayer. When she is called to investigate a fight in a bar right on the border between two of the most powerful groups in Atlanta it seems like a regular assignment, only it turns out to be anything but. Kate also has </span>
  <span id="freeText5908862496319312852" style="display:none">Buddy read with <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/5600230-armina" rel="nofollow noopener">Armina</a>, <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/17237503-eilonwy" rel="nofollow noopener">Eilonwy</a>, <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/3328287-asya" rel="nofollow noopener">Asya</a>, and <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/22911953-monty-cupcake" rel="nofollow noopener">Monty Cupcake</a>.<br /><br />Kate Daniels, an expert swordswoman works for the Order of Knights - an organization which solves magic problems. Kate does her solving part by chopping the given problem into small pieces with her sword appropriately called Slayer. When she is called to investigate a fight in a bar right on the border between two of the most powerful groups in Atlanta it seems like a regular assignment, only it turns out to be anything but. Kate also has a lot of personal problems at the moment which adds to the problem.<br /><br />At this time I really have to apologize as I am about to get into a rambling mode, but in this instance I cannot help it. The author(s) mentioned it was a very difficult book for her (them?) to write. Guess what - it shows. To increase a page count (this was my impression) one of the most abused (if not <b>the</b> most abused) cliche of romance genre was invoked. Imagine the following situation: a girl and a guy have a date; the guy does not show up. What would a normal human being (the one from real life) do as the girl in question? Try to get in touch and see that the problem was. Dear girls, please do it; you will have plenty of time to get pissed off later if the guy turned out to be a jerk and just did not feel like going outside. There are some really good reasons for not coming, like being near death.<br /><br />Why did I talk so much about the problem above? It took Kate exactly half of the book (I counted) to resolve this problem - by simply talking to Curran. Poor guy had a lot of broken bones which constitutes a very good excuse for not coming in my book. Why do I have to suffer through 150 pages of Kate's emotional turmoil by her own making entirely? Folks, this is the sole reason the book almost getting 2.5 star rating from me.<br /><br />There are two minor reasons for an extra 0.5 of a star in the rating; taken individually they are not enough, but combined they are. The first one is the humor; while it presents in much lesser quantities considering Kate's dark emotions, it is still there. The second one is my general respect for the series; the monsters for the most part are not the standard variety, including the main villain. Speaking about the latter Kate could figure out his/her identity much earlier had she not been absorbed in her personal problems. Do not read the book's blurb as it gives the identity away.<br /><br />All in all this is the most disappointing book of the series so far which barely made it into 3 star rating. My disappointment with it does not mean I will stop reading the series; I still consider it to be a minor stumble. Dear authors, it is not for me to give you an advice, but if you feel like the book is a struggle to write, stop and reconsider the whole work as it is quite possible you do something wrong and the end result might be underwhelming. I can think of a number of examples of these. <br /><br />This review is a copy/paste of my BookLikes one: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://gene.booklikes.com/post/994585/the-weakest-book-of-the-series-so-far-period">http://gene.booklikes.com/post/994585...</a></span>
  <a data-text-id="5908862496319312852" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <span id="freeText9608559939149978892" style="display:none"><i>"You know you've read a good book when you turn the last page and feel a little as if you have lost a friend."<br />— Paul Sweeney</i><br /><br />Now I have no idea who Paul Sweeney is. I'm an illiterate, poorly educated plebeian - I admit it.<br /><br />I also ask the many Kate Daniels fans on my friends list to forgive me. I made you think, in my first review, that I wasn't really digging this series.<br /><br />I was wrong. So very, very wrong.<br /><br />I loved this series. I loved it so much. I know there's more to go but I wish it were out already. I can't wait to read more and when it finally does end for good, I will be devestated.<br /><br />Everybody was right, Curran mellowed a little bit but he never changed. I suppose, over time I just grew to accept him. He'll never top the list as my absolute favourite literary boy toy. I think Clayton may just always sit there with Barrons and a few others scattered around him, semi-naked and cooling their hot bodies on the beach sands as I walk among them...<br /><br />OKAY! Back on track! But I have a total girlcrush on Kate. I love and adore her! I love this world that Andrews has created and the writing with which she has crafted it.<br /><br />-Signed,<br /><br />The New Kate Daniels Fan Girl</span>

<div id="review_1062060038" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1062060038" />
    <a title="Choko" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/27962805-choko"><img alt="Choko" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1475642755p2/27962805.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1062060038?book_show_action=true">Sep 22, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Choko" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Choko" href="/user/show/27962805-choko">Choko</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/27962805-choko?shelf=ilona-andrews">ilona-andrews</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/27962805-choko?shelf=kick-ass-ladies">kick-ass-ladies</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/27962805-choko?shelf=urban-fantasy">urban-fantasy</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1062060038" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17508868005763034542"><b>*** 5 ***<br/><br/>The Great Kate Daniels Buddy Read/Reread of 2017 with the gang at Ilona Andrews Addicts (IAA)!</b><br/><br/><b>
  <i>"...“You slept with Curran and you didn’t tell me? I’m your best friend.”<br/>“It didn’t come up.”<br/>“How disappointing for you.”<br/>Ha-ha. “That’s not what I meant.” ..."</i>
</b><br/><br/>Well, how can anyone give this emotional and action steamroller less than five stars??? If you are a fan of the series and give this book anything else, than you must be missing something vital... To the rest of us, this book is known</span>
  <span id="freeText17508868005763034542" style="display:none"><b>*** 5 ***<br /><br />The Great Kate Daniels Buddy Read/Reread of 2017 with the gang at Ilona Andrews Addicts (IAA)!</b><br /><br /><b>
  <i>"...“You slept with Curran and you didn’t tell me? I’m your best friend.”<br />“It didn’t come up.”<br />“How disappointing for you.”<br />Ha-ha. “That’s not what I meant.” ..."</i>
</b><br /><br />Well, how can anyone give this emotional and action steamroller less than five stars??? If you are a fan of the series and give this book anything else, than you must be missing something vital... To the rest of us, this book is known as the one "they finally did it!". This is not a spoiler, just what all the IA readership has been waiting for now three books in a row... We all knew it was coming, we just didn't know when and how, and boy did we not get disappointed! It was one feral, raw, emotional and darn satisfying resolution of many tense moments and not very smart or mature hilarious mating dance... All of it happening while a very virulent forms of plagues bringing creature is unleashed on the city, together with something that scares the minds out of people and shifters alike, as well as weird undead attacking all the major clans, creeds and organizations, freaking the population as a whole out. And the culprit might be a close family member of Kate's. Ahhh, her family tree are such sweet people, all of them:) <br /><br /><b>
  <i>"..."“You'll lose."<br />"What makes you so sure?"<br />"You have no discipline. All you do is tear down shit down. My father is a bastard, but at least he builds things. You turn cities into smoking ruins and blunder about like some hyper child, smashing anything you see. And then you sit here and wonder, 'Why did all of my children turn out to be violet idiots? It's a mystery of nature,'.” ..."</i>
</b><br /><br />Kate and Curran, Andrea and Raphael, love seems to be in the air, but there are complications, as it is always the case with the Pack. There are so many politics and clan manipulations, your head would spin. I wanted to scream at some of the clan Alphas, since all of them are constantly in-fighting for power and position, making Kate's future as the Beast Lord's mate a position full of danger and some ass kissing too, which I am sure she feels much less comfortable with than the power challenges. <br /><br /><b>
  <i>"..."“I surveyed the rest of the Council and looked directly at Mahon. “Some of you know me. Some of you have seen me fight and some of you are my friends. Have your vote. But know this: if you come to remove me, come in force, because if you try to separate me from him, I will kill every single one of you. My hand won't shake. My aim won't falter. My face will be the last thing you‟ll see before you die.”<br /><br />I jammed the knife into the table and walked out.” ..."</i>
</b><br /><br />We lost a very favorite animal, but we also gained a big protector for Kate - an attack poodle!!!! He is ferocious and scares.... well, mostly scares all who are danger to his girl, unless they have something to eat, of course...<br /><br /><b>
  <i>"..."“I also stole a small yellow doughnut from the box of Duncan's doughnuts in the rec room and fed it to the attack poodle in my office. He made a great production of it. First, he growled at the doughnut, just to show it who was boss. Then he nudged it with his nose. Then he licked it, until finally he snagged it into his mouth and chomped it with great pleasure, dropping crumbs all over the carpet.” ..."</i>
</b><br /><br />Overall, this installment of the series is the best so far and the IA team are getting better with every book! I wholeheartedly recommend this and any series written by the two of them when you feel like some action with a heart and no stinginess when it comes to battles and toughness, but also some romance sprinkled throughout. A modern classic of the Urban Fantasy Genre!!!! <br /><br />Now I wish you all Happy Reading and many more wonderful books to come!!! <br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="17508868005763034542" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>
