<div id="review_60139860" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/60139860" />
    <a title="Shannon" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2016128-shannon"><img alt="Shannon" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1572638169p2/2016128.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/60139860?book_show_action=true">Jun 18, 2009</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Shannon" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Shannon" href="/user/show/2016128-shannon">Shannon</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2016128-shannon?shelf=shifters">shifters</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2016128-shannon?shelf=sexy-urban-fantasy">sexy-urban-fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2016128-shannon?shelf=owned">owned</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2016128-shannon?shelf=color-green">color-green</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2016128-shannon?shelf=werewolves">werewolves</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2016128-shannon?shelf=color-grey">color-grey</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2016128-shannon?shelf=vampires">vampires</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2016128-shannon?shelf=2010">2010</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2016128-shannon?shelf=bought-2010">bought-2010</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2016128-shannon?shelf=magic">magic</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer60139860" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer18027623990092041931">I ran the gamut of emotions while reading this book; first I was annoyed, then bored, sad, excited, and finally happy. What's interesting, now that I think about it, is that <b>my emotions ran parallel to what Kate was feeling at the time</b>, which I have to say is a pretty outstanding feat for an author. <br/><br/><b>I spent the better part of the novel pissed off alongside Kate.</b> The opening scene shows Kate waiting in her kitchen with the dinner she made cooling and her temper heating up. She thinks Curran stood</span>
  <span id="freeText18027623990092041931" style="display:none">I ran the gamut of emotions while reading this book; first I was annoyed, then bored, sad, excited, and finally happy. What's interesting, now that I think about it, is that <b>my emotions ran parallel to what Kate was feeling at the time</b>, which I have to say is a pretty outstanding feat for an author. <br /><br /><b>I spent the better part of the novel pissed off alongside Kate.</b> The opening scene shows Kate waiting in her kitchen with the dinner she made cooling and her temper heating up. She thinks Curran stood her up and when she calls the Keep looking for him she's told that he's busy and not to bother him. She's understandably pissed off. Her first thought is to drive out their and chew his head off, but then she decides that's what the old Kate would do and she's trying to be more responsible. So instead of fighting him, she decides to give him the silent treatment. Of course, Curran has a reason for not showing up for dinner, but there isn't a way for him to explain because she won't talk to him. He's pissed at her, she's pissed at him, and it's all based on a giant misunderstanding caused by someone else. <b>I really wanted them to just sit down and talk, but with their volatile personalities it was believable that they wouldn't be able to just calmly talk things out without destroying something first.</b><br /><br /><b>The main villain of this installment was brilliant.</b> She's strong, evil, and a threat to everything Kate holds dear. I honestly think there is only one other villain that will hold a candle to her, and he has yet to even grace the pages, except in name and backstory. The villain's henchmen though, were kind of weak. For some reason they didn't have the same creepiness as the vampires and without any sort of separate intelligence they were little more than puppets. Venom was disgusting though.<br /><br /><b>Kate of course, was fantastic.</b> She really is my favorite heroine and probably the one out of all the series I read that I can relate to the most. <br /><br /><b>A few more things I loved that I won't go too far into for fear of spoiling:</b><br />Catnip/Weight Bench/Glue<br />Grendel: I love that Kate got a furry companion; even if his special power <i>is</i> throwing up on the floor. <br />I was especially glad with the choice she made in regards to the Order. <br />I hope she's finally done dealing with Saiman now, he sure is slimy<br />Naeemah, what she is and who she works for - duh, duh, DUH!<br />The council meeting - I actually said, "Fuck yeah, Kate!" out loud.<br />The end/epilogue<br /><br /><b>A few things that made me cry:</b><br />Kate finally coming clean with Curran and his reaction<br />Marigold : (<br />The attack on the wolves<br />The final fight<br /><br /><b>I could nitpick and point out the things that bothered me, but there really wasn't all that much.</b> Andrea kind of disappointed me. Some parts of the book were slow and at other times I was worried about where things were going to go so I'd set it aside for a few hours. And like I said, I was pissed off (mostly at Curran) because I agreed with Kate, but the end really fixed everything. <br /><br /><b>Also, it's plain to see that the authors are really setting up things for the long haul and that's not something I'm disappointed by.</b> I just hope they don't drag out this thing with Roland indefinitely and drive the series into the ground, but I always look forward to whatever they write.<br /><br />Check out my reviews of books two and three in this series: <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/45911879" rel="nofollow noopener">Magic Burns</a> and <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/45913706" rel="nofollow noopener">Magic Strikes</a>.</span>
  <a data-text-id="18027623990092041931" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_2646433725" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2646433725" />
    <a title="Ginger" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/14097149-ginger"><img alt="Ginger" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1593449448p2/14097149.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2646433725?book_show_action=true">Jan 28, 2020</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Ginger" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Ginger" href="/user/show/14097149-ginger">Ginger</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14097149-ginger?shelf=2020">2020</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2646433725" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3957757512890795107"><b>4.5 stars rounded up to 5 stars!</b><br/><br/>I stayed up way too late finishing this book. I’m going to suffer at work tomorrow! 🥴🤣<br/>This is always the sign of a good book when you can’t put it down and finish it in days.<br/><br/><b>Magic Bleeds</b> did this to me. This is the 4th book in the <i>Kate Daniels</i> series and I knew that I would enjoy it. I’ve enjoyed all the books in the series so far!<br/><br/>What I did not realize was how much I missed this series and characters. <i>Ilona Andrews</i> has created a kick ass heroine that most everyon</span>
  <span id="freeText3957757512890795107" style="display:none"><b>4.5 stars rounded up to 5 stars!</b><br><br>I stayed up way too late finishing this book. I’m going to suffer at work tomorrow! 🥴🤣<br>This is always the sign of a good book when you can’t put it down and finish it in days.<br><br><b>Magic Bleeds</b> did this to me. This is the 4th book in the <i>Kate Daniels</i> series and I knew that I would enjoy it. I’ve enjoyed all the books in the series so far!<br><br>What I did not realize was how much I missed this series and characters. <i>Ilona Andrews</i> has created a kick ass heroine that most everyone can cheer for. She’s tough, competent, loyal and snarky. In my opinion, the best kind!<br><br><b>Magic Bleeds</b> starts off with Kate investigating a fight and murder that happens at a neutral spot between the shapeshifters and necromancers.<br>A shapeshifter was killed in a gruesome way and ends up involving the Biohazard unit with the Order of the Knights.<br><br>Why was this shapeshifter killed and does it involve Kate’s father or are the necromancers doing this?<br><br><b>Magic Bleeds</b> continues with the hidden history of Kate Daniels and her heritage. I’m really enjoying where the series is going on this plot. We not only get more information about Roland, but we get to see where Kate and Curran’s relationship is taken.<br><br>Yeah, that was entertaining and <b>steamy</b>!<br><br>The only gripe that I had with <b>Magic Bleeds</b> was the lack of communication that happened with Kate and Curran in the beginning.<br>Ugh…must there always be drama with not talking to someone?!<br><br>Another great subplot in the book was reading and experiencing all the shapeshifter politics with the alphas and different beast clans.<br>It gives the series and shapeshifter community more interest and plots for further books!<br><br>One last thing that's great in <b>Magic Bleeds</b>, there’s an <b>attack poodle</b> in it!<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1580315919i/28864500._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>If you are looking for a great urban fantasy series to read, check out <i>Kate Daniels</i>. You won’t regret it!</span>
  <a data-text-id="3957757512890795107" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_153661540" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/153661540" />
    <a title="Jen Davis" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4669344-jen-davis"><img alt="Jen Davis" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1548427639p2/4669344.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/153661540?book_show_action=true">Mar 11, 2011</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jen Davis" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jen Davis" href="/user/show/4669344-jen-davis">Jen Davis</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>


          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">Any fan of Urban Fantasy</span></div>

        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4669344-jen-davis?shelf=kate-daniels">kate-daniels</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4669344-jen-davis?shelf=urban-fantasy">urban-fantasy</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer153661540" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer18012249215564397452">Let's take a moment to review the things I love in this life. <br/><br/><br/>*My husband and kids <br/><a href='http://s1092.photobucket.com/albums/i405/JenMartin1/?action=view&current=fam.jpg' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380346824i/701239.jpg' alt='Photobucket' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>*Diet Coke<br/><a href='http://s1092.photobucket.com/albums/i405/JenMartin1/?action=view&current=dc.jpg' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380346824i/701240.jpg' alt='Photobucket' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a> <br/><br/>*French Fries<br/><a href='http://s1092.photobucket.com/albums/i405/JenMartin1/?action=view&current=fries.jpg' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380346824i/701241.jpg' alt='Photobucket' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>*And an awesome little book, called <i>Magic Bleeds</i>. <br/><br/>I really didn't think the Kate Daniels series could actually get any better after <i>Magic Strikes</i>. But as good as that one was, this one was better.<br/><br/>As the book begins, Kate is preparing for that naked dinner she promised Curran. But he doesn't show. She calls The Keep and gets the brush off. And hours later, she decides she's been </span>
  <span id="freeText18012249215564397452" style="display:none">Let's take a moment to review the things I love in this life. <br><br><br>*My husband and kids <br><a href="http://s1092.photobucket.com/albums/i405/JenMartin1/?action=view&amp;current=fam.jpg" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380346824i/701239.jpg" alt="Photobucket" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>*Diet Coke<br><a href="http://s1092.photobucket.com/albums/i405/JenMartin1/?action=view&amp;current=dc.jpg" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380346824i/701240.jpg" alt="Photobucket" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> <br><br>*French Fries<br><a href="http://s1092.photobucket.com/albums/i405/JenMartin1/?action=view&amp;current=fries.jpg" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380346824i/701241.jpg" alt="Photobucket" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>*And an awesome little book, called <i>Magic Bleeds</i>. <br><br>I really didn't think the Kate Daniels series could actually get any better after <i>Magic Strikes</i>. But as good as that one was, this one was better.<br><br>As the book begins, Kate is preparing for that naked dinner she promised Curran. But he doesn't show. She calls The Keep and gets the brush off. And hours later, she decides she's been played for a fool. A few weeks later, she is back at work and determined to forget her feelings for the Beast Lord. She gets pulled into a case, where a mysterious being is bringing a plague to Atlanta. Throughout the course of the investigation, Kate has to use her contacts with the mercenary guild, Saiman, and even the shapeshifters. Which throws her plan to avoid Curran out of the window.<br><br>It's clear these two are crazy about each other, but there's a lot working against them... The worst offenders are their responsibilities and stubbornness. But it is so gratifying to watch them work it out. Their relationship is so great, because they can retain their individual strengths, while allowing the other in. During their courtship, we learn a lot about Curran's background and pack politics. Not only that, we see what it will mean if Kate needs to carve herself a place in his life.<br><br>While Kate's personal life heats up, her investigation into the Plaguemaker takes a more personal turn. As so many things in her life do, it ends up with a major connection to Roland. And it forces her to share some of her most closely kept secrets.<br><br>AND THERE IS FINALLY SOME SEX. <br><br>I can't say enough about how good this book was. Not only does it put most other series to shame... It puts the first two books in this series to shame as well. All hail Kate Daniels. 5 stars.<br><br><br></span>

<div id="review_994340196" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/994340196" />
    <a title="ȷαεlα" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/16126654-l"><img alt="ȷαεlα" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1589706072p2/16126654.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/994340196?book_show_action=true">Jul 12, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="ȷαεlα" class="user" itemprop="url" name="ȷαεlα" href="/user/show/16126654-l">ȷαεlα</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer994340196" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14050687434899779252"><b>First read July 2014<br/>Second read May 2016</b><br/><br/>Rating: Same. (I'll explain)<br/><br/>This book is called Magic Bleeds. Just like my heart bled for Kate in the first chapters. <br/><br/><b>For years, first my father and then my guardian, Greg, had warned me to stay away from human relationships. Friends and lovers only brought you trouble.<br/><br/>...................................................................<br/><br/>One day I’d find someone to lean on as well. It just wouldn’t be Curran. And I really had to stop thinking about him, becau</b></span>
  <span id="freeText14050687434899779252" style="display:none"><b>First read July 2014<br>Second read May 2016</b><br><br>Rating: Same. (I'll explain)<br><br>This book is called Magic Bleeds. Just like my heart bled for Kate in the first chapters. <br><br><b>For years, first my father and then my guardian, Greg, had warned me to stay away from human relationships. Friends and lovers only brought you trouble.<br><br>...................................................................<br><br>One day I’d find someone to lean on as well. It just wouldn’t be Curran. And I really had to stop thinking about him, because it hurt.</b><br><br>When you don't know what's really happening, don't you just want to kill Curran?? How could he do that to poor Kate??<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1452792854ra/17744531.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Curran likes to play. He's a cat after all. a big one, but still a cat. He is attracted to power, which Kate has in large quantities. I think he was cynical in this book. Even his thoughts were cynical (<a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/20295040.Curran_POV_Collection" title="Curran POV Collection by Gordon Andrews" rel="nofollow noopener">Curran POV Collection</a>). He wants Kate, but he's not eager to sacrifice anything. He demands things from Kate and gives nothing in return, because he's <i>the Beast Lord</i>. <br><br>One of the best parts of the book was the Conclave scene. Oh, how I loved Saiman there. I was enjoying so much that Curran was suffering.<br><br><b>
  <i>“There is only one difference between us. The Beast Lord will lie to you. He’ll tell you he loves you, that you’ll always be the only one, that he’ll sacrifice everything to be with you and keep you safe. I won’t lie to you. I won’t make promises I can’t keep. Honesty, Kate. I offer honesty.”</i>
</b><br><br>I couldn't agree more. This. <b>THIS</b> is the reason for my disbelief towards Curran. Take it, you jerk!<br><br>And the other best part was when Kate massacred all her challengers. She is a total kickass/badass.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1462719628i/19034966.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Of course there were some <i>steeamyyy</i> scenes, that uhhh...<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1462719628ra/19034967.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>And the humor is never absent:<br><br><b>
  <i> “While you’re with me, I’m the only one. Anybody else touches you and I’ll kill them.”<br>“What if I accidentally bump into someone?”<br>Gold flashed in his eyes. “Don’t.”</i>
</b><br><br><i>4 **** stars</i>, because:<br><br><b>
  <i>"Besides, if Curran didn't think you're fit, he wouldn't have made the offer. Yes, he's obsessed with you, but he's shrewd enough to take your ability into consideration. Alphas are typically attracted to other alphas. I wouldn't mate with a weakling, and neither would he. </i>
</b><br><br>This part, and oh so many others, make me think that the only reason Curran wants Kate is so she can help him protect his <i>damn Pack</i>. So you can understand now why I started liking him only at the end of book #7 and in book #8. <br><br>Nevertheless, the book was full of good action. Secondary characters make this book awesome. Dr Doolittle is so funny. Have you guys noticed the age difference between Julie and Derek is 6 years, same as in Kate/Curran? I should have noticed these hints!<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1462719628ra/19034968.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>
  <a data-text-id="14050687434899779252" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_550569474" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/550569474" />
    <a title="Angela" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4255477-angela"><img alt="Angela" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1398251387p2/4255477.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/550569474?book_show_action=true">Mar 02, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Angela" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Angela" href="/user/show/4255477-angela">Angela</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/9657611-magic-bleeds">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4255477-angela?shelf=2016-read">2016-read</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4255477-angela?shelf=urban-fantasy">urban-fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4255477-angela?shelf=2015-read">2015-read</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4255477-angela?shelf=kindle">kindle</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4255477-angela?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4255477-angela?shelf=2014-read">2014-read</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4255477-angela?shelf=2018-read">2018-read</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer550569474" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17133287701077241503">June 2016 Re-read.<br/><br/>09/2015 Re-read: How is it possible that I just continue to love this series more and more and more with every reading?<br/><br/><br/>This series has some of the shortest blurbs I've ever read. After the end of <i>Magic Strikes</i>, I was so eager to start this book. It seemed like <b>finally</b> everything we'd been waiting for between Curran and Kate was going to happen.<br/><br/>And then I sat, alongside Kate, as it all came shattering down. Curran didn't show. Curran didn't take her call. Kate was hurt, and deva</span>
  <span id="freeText17133287701077241503" style="display:none">June 2016 Re-read.<br /><br />09/2015 Re-read: How is it possible that I just continue to love this series more and more and more with every reading?<br /><br /><br />This series has some of the shortest blurbs I've ever read. After the end of <i>Magic Strikes</i>, I was so eager to start this book. It seemed like <b>finally</b> everything we'd been waiting for between Curran and Kate was going to happen.<br /><br />And then I sat, alongside Kate, as it all came shattering down. Curran didn't show. Curran didn't take her call. Kate was hurt, and devastated, and then she got mad. I was right there with her. <br /><br />It's hard to talk about this book without a lot of spoilers. The plot - again - is tightly written and the pacing is spot on. I could hardly catch my breath while I read. Everyone got in on the action here - the Masters of the Dead, the shapeshifters, the Order and the Guild - no one was safe. <br /><br />And then there's the villain. So utterly perfect, and terrifying. The stakes keeping getting ramped up, and the opponents keep getting more difficult to deal with. Ilona Andrews is doing a superb job of ratcheting up the suspense in the lead up to what we all know has to come eventually for Kate; the thing she's been training her whole life for.<br /><br />Though I didn't get the payout I wanted at the beginning of <i>Magic Bleeds</i>, I definitely got satisfaction. Watching Kate and Curran circle each other, tease each other, and go through their own mating ritual made me grin, laugh out loud, and so incredibly happy when they finally figured out how to make it work.<br /><br />The final showdown, I can't even begin to talk about, but it had me on the edge of my seat. Then when it was done, they went and ripped my heart out, stomped on it a couple of times, and handed me back the mushy remains.<br /><br /><i>Magic Bleeds</i> proves that Ilona Andrews is in top form. These books just get better on re-reads, and I love going back to visit with all of the beloved characters.<br /><br /><br />20 July 2014: <a href="http://www.amazon.com/gp/product/B003NX7NHO/ref=as_li_tl?ie=UTF8&amp;camp=1789&amp;creative=390957&amp;creativeASIN=B003NX7NHO&amp;linkCode=as2&amp;tag=touthenig-20&amp;linkId=VI5S27LSWM4FXKJE" rel="nofollow noopener">$1.99 on Kindle</a><br /><br />This is my favorite series ever!!! And the whole series is on sale!</span>
  <a data-text-id="17133287701077241503" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

<span id="freeTextContainer6619748591417422608">One of my favorite in the series!<br/><br/>If you got to the 4th book then there is no need for me to tell you to read this. If you haven't read any of Kate Daniels' books and you like Urban Fantasy than what are you waiting for?<br/><br/>What I liked about this particular novel was that we finally meet a member of the Kate's family. I kind of liked her aunt even if she was supposed to be the villain. There were some power games between Curran and Kate, some entertaining, some annoying. <br/><br/></span>

<div id="review_1545389051" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1545389051" />
    <a title="Simona B" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5312173-simona-b"><img alt="Simona B" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1408893128p2/5312173.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1545389051?book_show_action=true">Feb 11, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Simona B" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Simona B" href="/user/show/5312173-simona-b">Simona B</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5312173-simona-b?shelf=2000">2000</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5312173-simona-b?shelf=in-english">in-english</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5312173-simona-b?shelf=fantastic-lit-and-co">fantastic-lit-and-co</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5312173-simona-b?shelf=ebooks">ebooks</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1545389051" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9049009471460652655"><b>"Just wait until he figures out I shut him out of his slut hut."</b><br/><br/>You know in <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1544432951?book_show_action=false' rel='nofollow noopener'>my review of <i>Magic Strikes</i></a> when I said that Kate and Curran are <b>frustratingly cute</b>? Well, that's strange. It's strange because before reading <i>Magic Bleeds</i> I didn't and couldn't have the slightest idea of what this expression actually means. <br/><br/>•If Kate and Curran were frustratingly cute before, now they are <b>excruciatingly adorable</b>. Their on-off relationship will drive you out of your mind, the tension between them is -posit</span>
  <span id="freeText9049009471460652655" style="display:none"><b>"Just wait until he figures out I shut him out of his slut hut."</b><br /><br />You know in <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1544432951?book_show_action=false" rel="nofollow noopener">my review of <i>Magic Strikes</i></a> when I said that Kate and Curran are <b>frustratingly cute</b>? Well, that's strange. It's strange because before reading <i>Magic Bleeds</i> I didn't and couldn't have the slightest idea of what this expression actually means. <br /><br />•If Kate and Curran were frustratingly cute before, now they are <b>excruciatingly adorable</b>. Their on-off relationship will drive you out of your mind, the tension between them is -positively- unbearable, and the <b>chemistry </b>is<b> sky-high</b>. <br /><br />•In this regard, <b>Kate</b> is begginig to show a <b>considerable development</b>. She must learn to deal with her past, her education, she must accept the kind of person she want to be in relation with the kind of warrior her stepfather wanted her to become, and find a balance between the two. It's lovely to see how <b>her life changed</b> from book one up to now, how she passed from being a solitary creature to being surrounded by so many caring people and how she adapted to this. It's like I can physically see her characters grow and develop and evolve in front of my eyes, and given how much I take the characters into account when rating a book, this played a key role in my enjoyment.<br /><br />•The <b>plot</b> is maybe less crucial (as I said, the book is mainly centered about the characters), but surely as <b>captivating</b> as <i>Magic Strike</i>'s was, and once again the<b> balance </b>between the most introspective parts and the most fast-paced and action-packed ones was <b>absolutely satisfying</b>, a great improvement compared to book one and two, where in comparison the characters were practically invisible.<br /><br />•<b>Curran</b>. I have nothing specific to say about him, but I thought I ought to name a paragraph after him. So, <b>Curran</b>. I just asked my parents for a <b>Curran</b> all mine and they said they'll begin to save some money. If you want to contribute, I can give you their number. Just gift me a <b>Curran</b>. <b>Curran</b>. You see how nice his name is? (Not only the name, ahem). So pleasant to pronounce. <b>Curraaaaaan</b>. <b> Cur-ra-an</b>. <br /><br />(I can't believe I'm Lolitaing him... and I can't believe I used Lolita as a verb.)<br /><br />Ok, ok, I'll stop now. Sorry. But <b>Curran</b>-<br /><br />*keeps obsessing and talking to herself <i>ad libitum</i>*</span>

          </span>

<div id="review_2163586286" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2163586286" />
    <a title="Geri Reads" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/11757728-geri-reads"><img alt="Geri Reads" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1487874758p2/11757728.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2163586286?book_show_action=true">Oct 25, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Geri Reads" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Geri Reads" href="/user/show/11757728-geri-reads">Geri Reads</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11757728-geri-reads?shelf=all-my-loves">all-my-loves</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2163586286" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8415424778520814367"><b>Re-read! Rating still stands!</b><br/><br/><b>
  <blockquote>“I can't give you the white picket fence, and if I did, you'd set it on fire.”</blockquote>
</b><br/><br/>What can I say? AnotheramazinginstallmentintheKateDanielsseries!!!<br/><br/>Kate Daniels, mercenary and psuedo Knight of the order gets to meet a long lost family member. It should've been a happy family reunion but this is Kate Daniels we're talking about and to say that her family is just dysfunctional is an UNDERSTATEMENT!<br/><br/>The stakes just keeps getting higher and Kate is confronting bigger and </span>
  <span id="freeText8415424778520814367" style="display:none"><b>Re-read! Rating still stands!</b><br><br><b>
  <blockquote>“I can't give you the white picket fence, and if I did, you'd set it on fire.”</blockquote>
</b><br><br>What can I say? AnotheramazinginstallmentintheKateDanielsseries!!!<br><br>Kate Daniels, mercenary and psuedo Knight of the order gets to meet a long lost family member. It should've been a happy family reunion but this is Kate Daniels we're talking about and to say that her family is just dysfunctional is an UNDERSTATEMENT!<br><br>The stakes just keeps getting higher and Kate is confronting bigger and more powerful beings. Man, the action in this book is top notch. There are so many moments where I don't even know if Kate and Curran would come out of it alive. <br><br><b>
  <blockquote>“Don’t die on me, you stupid sonovabitch. You goddamn fucking idiot. I told you to stay out of the damn fight! Why the hell don’t you ever listen? I fucking hate you. I hate you, you hear me? Don’t you dare die on me, because I need to kill you with my bare hands.”</blockquote>
</b> <br><br>There's also politics and intrigue added to the mix. In the hands of less skilled writers, this book would've feel bloated but Gordon and Ilona have proven themselves adept at juggling storylines. But where they really shine is with their characters. <br><br>Again, we see growth with each and every character in this series. Kate has changed. She's still Kate but with each and every book, we get to see her make tough decisions. There's a really powerful scene in this book where we see Kate struggle with a decision between doing what she was taught to do and doing what was right. That scene was so powerful to me because it speaks of who Kate is and I know I sound like a broken record here but man, she's such an amazing hero. <br><br><b>
  <blockquote>“The stairs ended. I wished I knew the jackass who’d made the staircase so short. I’d throw him down the damn steps so he could count them with his head.”</blockquote>
</b> <br><br>But what really makes this book special is the romance department. Look, I'm not one of those people who thinks that a badass heroine becomes less of a badass because she wants love or falls in love with the hero. Nope. I'm firmly in the "heroines can fall in love and still be a badass because we can do whatever the fuck we want" camp. And Kate does what she wants. And she wants the Beast Lord. And I can totally get behind that because while Curran might be overbearing at times, he is learning and making comprises with Kate. <br><br><b>
  <blockquote>“You might want to decide fast. We live in a dangerous world. If you see a chance to be happy, you have to fight for it, so later you have no regrets.”</blockquote>
</b> <br><br>I love how they negotiated and compromised with each other. They are both stubborn. Both are alpha. Kate has baggage, so does Curran and they both have identities outside of each other. Curran's life is with the pack, while Kate was a loner. She doesn't belong to anyone. It would've been a disservice to Kate's character if she suddenly becomes subservient to Curran and vice versa. But somehow Ilona Andrews made it work. That doesn't mean they didn't make mistakes. They made plenty of mistakes. They had their share of jealous fits and misunderstanding but the way the authors handled their conflict was wonderful. <br><br><b>
  <blockquote>Mad gold eyes stared into mine. "Do you miss me, Kate?"<br>I closed my eyes trying to shut him out. I could lie then we would be back to square one. Nothing would be resolved. I'd still be alone, hating him and wanting him.<br>He grabbed my shoulders and shook me once. "Do you miss me?"<br>I took the plunge. "Yes.”</blockquote>
</b><br><br>I've never read 4 straight books in a series before. Never. I tend to get bored easily even with series I love. But this is just too good to put down. So I'm off to read book 5. <br><br><b>
  <blockquote>“I gave him my hard stare. “You're a control freak and I fight all authority. And you want us to mate?”<br>A wicked spark lit his eyes. “Many, many times.”</blockquote>
</b><br><br>________________________________<br><a href="http://tinypic.com?ref=212u179" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1508936976ra/24268263.gif" alt="Image and video hosting by TinyPic" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a></span>
  <a data-text-id="8415424778520814367" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1017867882" />
    <a title="Anne" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/1720620-anne"><img alt="Anne" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1415374035p2/1720620.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Anne" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Anne" href="/user/show/1720620-anne">Anne</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1720620-anne?shelf=kindle">kindle</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1017867882" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11623634452940015370">4.5 stars<br/><br/>This book probably saved my sanity. Really.<br/>We went <i>camping</i> a few days ago. And I hate camping even when everything goes perfectly. This time, the boys and I got a stomach bug.<br/>It wasn't one of those debilitating bugs, unfortunately, because <i>then</i> we could have left. <br/>No.<br/>It was just one of those bugs that made you 'uncomfortable'.<br/><i>1:00 am<br/><b>*ACHOO!*</b><br/>Moooooom!!!!<br/>I <b>sharted</b>!</i><br/>Do you have <i>any</i> idea what it's like to have to walk a kid (<i>who has shit in their pants</i>) down to a woodsy 'bathhouse' at 1:00 i</span>
  <span id="freeText11623634452940015370" style="display:none">4.5 stars<br /><br />This book probably saved my sanity. Really.<br />We went <i>camping</i> a few days ago. And I hate camping even when everything goes perfectly. This time, the boys and I got a stomach bug.<br />It wasn't one of those debilitating bugs, unfortunately, because <i>then</i> we could have left. <br />No.<br />It was just one of those bugs that made you 'uncomfortable'.<br /><i>1:00 am<br /><b>*ACHOO!*</b><br />Moooooom!!!!<br />I <b>sharted</b>!</i><br />Do you have <i>any</i> idea what it's like to have to walk a kid (<i>who has shit in their pants</i>) down to a woodsy 'bathhouse' at 1:00 in the morning?<br />Only to have them realize (<i>far too late to get new PJs</i>) that the liquid they expelled has drizzled into their pajama pants?<br />Now imagine that same kid running full-tilt back to the camper, in the dark, through the woods, squealing, in nothing but their (<i>new/clean</i>) underwear.<br />My poor kid is still having nightmares about the hysterical laughter that trailed them back to safety.<br /><i>Sorry, baby. I get a little slap-happy when I've had no sleep. Also, it was just damn funny to watch you crash through the brush like your little ass was on fire.</i> <br />But beyond my nightly entertainment, there wasn't much to do. It's not like we could chance a hike. Upset tummies don't mix well with long treks away from the potty.<br />So. The boys and I sat in the camper. <br /><i>
  <b>Fun Fact:</b>
</i><br />Boys have a shelf life of about 8 hours, before they start to smell really bad.<br /><br />So. Thank you, Kate, for allowing me to mentally escape from my family vacation.<br /><br /><i>
  <b>Oh My GAWD!</b>
</i><br /><br />This is <i>it</i>, people! Book 4 is the one where they <i>finally</i>...<br />Is it a spoiler if I say it out loud?<br /><i>*bites nails*</i><br />Hmm. I'm not sure, to be quite honest. <b>But</b>, for those of you who know what I'm talking about? <br /><i>*squee!*</i><br /><br />Alrighty, this book isn't just amazing because of the <i>thing</i>. There's also a whole lotta action 'n suspense stuff to go along with it. Kate meets up with her <b>
  <i>eeeevil</i>
</b> aunt!<br />OMG! How will this effect her future?! Will Roland find her now?! Will the Pack be a bigger target?! What about Julie?!<br /><i>I'm using too many exclamation points, aren't I?</i><br /><br />I'm not sure how to describe how <i>into</i> these books I am right now. <br />I. Can't. Stop.<br />In fact, I've already checked out the next book from my library.<br />Oh! Oh! There's an <b>attack poodle</b> in this one!<br />How can you resist a series that has an attack poodle?!<br />You can't! No one could resist <i>that</i>!<br /><br />I haven't found any UF series that I liked as much a my beloved <b>Mercy Thompson</b>, but <b>Kate Daniels</b> is a <i>very</i> close second, at this point. If you're looking for a kick-ass heroine, no weird sex <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ and by that, I mean they don't bite each other in odd places <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>, and a lot of interesting characters, then you might want to start on this series right away.<br /><br /><br /></span>

    <div class="section">
      

<div id="review_200481479" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/200481479" />
    <a title="Lora" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4632071-lora"><img alt="Lora" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1305237530p2/4632071.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/200481479?book_show_action=true">Aug 20, 2011</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Lora" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Lora" href="/user/show/4632071-lora">Lora</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>


          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">fans of the previous books</span></div>

        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4632071-lora?shelf=lib-read">lib-read</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4632071-lora?shelf=urban-fantasy">urban-fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4632071-lora?shelf=series-still-follow">series-still-follow</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer200481479" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16178388006719484933">While the covers never cease being hideous, each installment in the Kate Daniels series hasn't ceased to entertain me thus far. The fourth installment, <i>Magic Bleeds</i>, features a crocodile shapeshifter, a splendid impersonation of Mr. and Mrs. Smith, and a battle to end all battles. It is one hell of a ride.<br/><br/>I think one of the best things about this series is that it is appealing to both genders. It has lots of action, which of course men like, but I think I speak for all women when I say that we l</span>
  <span id="freeText16178388006719484933" style="display:none">While the covers never cease being hideous, each installment in the Kate Daniels series hasn't ceased to entertain me thus far. The fourth installment, <i>Magic Bleeds</i>, features a crocodile shapeshifter, a splendid impersonation of Mr. and Mrs. Smith, and a battle to end all battles. It is one hell of a ride.<br /><br />I think one of the best things about this series is that it is appealing to both genders. It has lots of action, which of course men like, but I think I speak for all women when I say that we like action, too. It keeps things interesting and wards off dullness. There's also just the right amount of romance. Not so much that would make guys squeamish, but still enough to keep the ladies satisfied. <br />And, while I think the first book was slightly lacking in this area, the humor is now on par with my taste as well. Kate seems to have better quips with each installment and never looses her nerve, even with Curran. And the banter and antics between Kate and Curran are sure to entertain most readers.<br /><br />I have theories on some of the reasons why Kate and Curran are attracted to each other. I think Kate likes Curran because he's one of the few people who could take her in a fight. Imagine if every guy you met you were superior to in fighting skills and he couldn't even win against you in a late-night arm wrestle. I'm sure there are plenty of women who enjoy being the stronger of the two in their relationship, but I don't believe that's the kind of relationship Kate wants. That is just one of the many reasons why Kate and Crest never would have worked out. I think Curran makes Kate feel like a woman for the first time in a long time.<br />And although he'd probably never admit it, I believe Curran's attracted to Kate because she doesn't take any of his shit. Unlike everyone else in his life, she doesn't bow to him, literally or figuratively. I think, secretly, the Beast Lord wants someone to treat him like a normal man, like he's just another person, even if only in private. At times, Curran and Kate collide like fire and kerosene - but they truly fit together like two matching jigsaw pieces.<br /><br />And do I smell a potential spin-off series in the oven? Granted, the buzzer won't go off for at least a couple of years, but when it does it'll surely be some good eatin'! Here's my reasoning: In <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/4345498.Magic_Strikes__Kate_Daniels___3_" title="Magic Strikes (Kate Daniels, #3) by Ilona Andrews" rel="nofollow noopener">Magic Strikes</a> we find out through a conversation that Kate was nine when Curran was fifteen and made Lord of all Beasts. This, of course, tells us that Curran is six years older than Kate. Well, we know that Julie and Derek are thirteen and nineteen, respectively, as of now. Do you see where I'm going with this? Once Julie gets older, her and Derek could have their own series! Her abilities coupled with the adolescent attraction she currently has for Derek could really make for an interesting future series. . . .<br /><br />I'll be honest: people with weak stomachs may not be able to stomach some of the talk of entrails and the bloody descriptions in this series. With lots of action comes lots of violence and gore. Normally that sort of thing would bother me, but I've gotten so used to it with this series that I don't even notice anymore. Plus it just seems to fit with this world.<br /><br />I'm actually feeling a little sad now because I know that once I finish the next installment, <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/8559047.Magic_Slays__Kate_Daniels___5_" title="Magic Slays (Kate Daniels, #5) by Ilona Andrews" rel="nofollow noopener">Magic Slays</a>, that'll be it until February of 2013 when the next book is released. I've quickly become addicted to this series and I'm reluctant to leave it.<br /><br />P.S. But, luckily, Andrews won't leave us hanging until then! For the full info, go <a href="http://www.ilona-andrews.com/2011/08/04/something-funny-happened-on-the-way-to-mass-market/" rel="nofollow noopener">here</a>.<br /><br />**************************************************************<br /><br /><b>My reviews of other titles in this series:</b><br /><br />Book #1 - <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/194889805" rel="nofollow noopener">Magic Bites</a><br />Book #2 - <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/197030282" rel="nofollow noopener">Magic Burns</a><br />Book #3 - <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/198478924" rel="nofollow noopener">Magic Strikes</a></span>
  <a data-text-id="16178388006719484933" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('94HUuu18XS09yFHiUbtpXqUNPACRnBY5D1O5XQAA/hHGbbxiDfv7ydeRCy7VooJ/cZ0wlZtcXmFt2MikYyTSzw==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('eZRnOiOywvrtDk+Qf4zaw32mOpsZUDntJAbUiCW2JyZIeA/iwzVkHgdXFVz7lTHiqTY2DhOQcbVGjaVxRpIL+A==')})
  }

<div class='bookAuthorProfile__about'>

<span id="freeTextContainer2142470447359369309">Ilona Andrews is the pseudonym for a husband-and-wife writing team. Ilona is a native-born Russian and Gordon is a former communications sergeant in the U.S. Army. Contrary to popular belief, Gordon was never an intelligence officer with a license to kill, and Ilona was never the mysterious Russian spy who seduced him. They met in college, in English Composition 101, where Ilona got a better grade</span>
  <span id="freeText2142470447359369309" style="display:none">Ilona Andrews is the pseudonym for a husband-and-wife writing team. Ilona is a native-born Russian and Gordon is a former communications sergeant in the U.S. Army. Contrary to popular belief, Gordon was never an intelligence officer with a license to kill, and Ilona was never the mysterious Russian spy who seduced him. They met in college, in English Composition 101, where Ilona got a better grade. (Gordon is still sore about that.)<br /><br />Gordon and Ilona currently reside in Oregon with their two children, three dogs and a cat. They have co-authored two series, the bestselling urban fantasy of Kate Daniels and romantic urban fantasy of The Edge.<br /></span>
